namespace = roc_subculture
########################################
#Sub-culture splits from Primary Culture
########################################

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.1
	title = roc_subculture.1.t
	desc = roc_subculture.1.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = pommeranian
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pommeranian
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pommeranian
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = pommeranian
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pommeranian
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = pommeranian
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = pommeranian
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = pommeranian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = austrian
				}
			}
		}

			if = {

					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = austrian
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = austrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.11.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}

					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = english
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = british
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = english
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = english
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2

				culture = english
			}
		}

							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = english
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = english

	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = venetian
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = venetian
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = venetian
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = latin
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = venetian
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = venetian
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = venetian
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = venetian
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = venetian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.35.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

				}

				}
			}

			}
		}
		owner = {

				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}

			NOT = {
				primary_culture = catalan
			}
		}

				}

			}

		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = slovene
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = slovene
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = slovene
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = south_slavic
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = slovene
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = slovene
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = slovene
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = slovene
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = slovene
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.71.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.83
	title = roc_subculture.83.t
	desc = roc_subculture.83.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = russian
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = russian
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = russian
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = east_slavic
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = russian
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = russian
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = russian
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = russian
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = russian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.83.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = slavic
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = czech_new
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = czech_new
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = czech_new
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = czech_new
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = czech_new
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.94.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.106
	title = roc_subculture.106.t
	desc = roc_subculture.106.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = greek
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = greek
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = greek
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = byzantine
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = greek
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = greek
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = greek
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = greek
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = greek
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.106.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = turko_semitic
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = al_suryah_arabic
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = al_suryah_arabic
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = al_suryah_arabic
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = al_suryah_arabic
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = al_suryah_arabic
			}
		}

		}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.128
	title = roc_subculture.128.t
	desc = roc_subculture.128.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = persian
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = persian
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = persian
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = iranian
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = persian
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = persian
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = persian
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = persian
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = persian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.128.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.151
	title = roc_subculture.151.t
	desc = roc_subculture.151.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = tepic
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = tepic
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = tepic
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = arido_american
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = tepic
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = tepic
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = tepic
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = tepic
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = tepic
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.151.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.152
	title = roc_subculture.152.t

				any_province = {

			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {

			culture_group = arido_american
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = chichimecan
			}
		}

			factor = 1
			NOT = {

				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}

	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.152.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {

							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = chontales
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = chontales
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			factor = 1
		}

				change_culture = maipurean
			}
		}

	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.185.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.186
	title = roc_subculture.186.t
	desc = roc_subculture.186.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = carib
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = carib
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = carib
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = carribean
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = carib
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = carib
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = carib
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = carib
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = carib
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.186.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = mesquakie
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = mesquakie
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = mesquakie
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = mesquakie
			}
		}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = pequot
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pequot
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pequot
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = eastern_algonquian
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = pequot
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = pequot
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = pequot
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = pequot
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = pequot
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.208.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = osage

							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = osage
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = osage
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			factor = 1
		}
	}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.243
	title = roc_subculture.243.t
	desc = roc_subculture.243.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = chinook
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = chinook
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = chinook
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = penutian
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = chinook
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = chinook
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = chinook
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = chinook
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = chinook
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.243.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = jianghuai
			}
		}

			NOT = {

						}

			}

			NOT = {

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = avadhi
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = avadhi
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.312.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.336
	title = roc_subculture.336.t
	desc = roc_subculture.336.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = dyola
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = dyola
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = dyola
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = mande
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = dyola
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = dyola
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = dyola
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = dyola
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = dyola
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.336.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = fon
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = fon
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.346.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = kongo_group
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = yaka
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = yaka
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = yaka
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = yaka
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = yaka
			}
		}

		}

province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.370
	title = roc_subculture.370.t
	desc = roc_subculture.370.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = bena
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = bena
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = bena
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = african
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = bena
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = bena
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = bena
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = bena
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = bena
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.370.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = nubian
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = roc_subculture.405
	title = roc_subculture.405.t
	desc = roc_subculture.405.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				any_province = {
					culture = joseon
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = joseon
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				had_country_flag = {  
					flag = new_subculture
					days = 1000
				}
			}
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = joseon
			}
		}
		owner = {
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				value = 10
				culture = ROOT
			}
			culture_group = koreang
			NOT = {
				primary_culture = joseon
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 200
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			NOT = { 
				any_neighbor_province = { 
					culture = joseon
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = joseon
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						had_country_flag = {
							flag = new_subculture
							days = 1500
						}
					}
				}
				change_culture = joseon
			}
			else_if = {
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = new_subculture
				}
				change_culture = joseon
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_subculture.405.a
		ai_chance = {			
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
